     1 // صفحة إدارة الحسابات المكررة وحظر الأجهزة

    21 
    22 function fmt(d?: string | null) {
    23   if (!d) return '—';
    24   try { return format(new Date(d), 'dd MMM yyyy HH:mm', { locale: ar }); }
    25   catch { return d; }
    26 }
    27 
    28 function shortFp(fp?: string | null) {
    29   if (!fp) return '—';
    30   return fp.length > 12 ? `${fp.slice(0, 6)}…${fp.slice(-6)}` : fp;

   189 // ── الصفحة الرئيسية ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
   190 export default function AdminDuplicateAccounts() {
   191   const navigate = useNavigate();
   192   const [tab, setTab] = useState<'duplicates' | 'bans'>('duplicates');
   193 
   194   const [dupes, setDupes]       = useState<DuplicateDeviceGroup[]>([]);
   195   const [bans,  setBans]        = useState<DeviceBan[]>([]);
   196   const [loading, setLoading]   = useState(true);
   197   const [search, setSearch]     = useState('');
   198   const [filterBanned, setFilterBanned] = useState<'all' | 'banned' | 'unbanned'>('all');
   199 
   200   // حوار الحظر
   201   const [banTarget, setBanTarget] = useState<DuplicateDeviceGroup | null>(null);
   202   const [banNote, setBanNote]     = useState('');
   203   const [banning, setBanning]     = useState(false);
   204 
   205   // حوار تأكيد رفع الحظر
   206   const [unbanId, setUnbanId]     = useState<string | null>(null);
   207   const [unbanning, setUnbanning] = useState(false);
   208 
   209   const load = useCallback(async () => {
   210     setLoading(true);
   211     try {
   212       const [d, b] = await Promise.all([getDuplicateDevices(), getDeviceBans()]);
   213       if (d.success) setDupes(d.data);
   214       else toast.error(d.error ?? 'فشل جلب الأجهزة المكررة');
   215       if (b.success) setBans(b.data);
   216     } finally { setLoading(false); }
   217   }, []);
   218 
   219   useEffect(() => { load(); }, [load]);
   220 
   221   const filteredDupes = dupes.filter(g => {
   222     const q = search.toLowerCase();
   223     const matchQ = !q ||
   224       (g.device_fp ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
   225       (g.device_id ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
   226       g.usernames.some(u => (u ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q)) ||
   227       g.phones.some(p => (p ?? '').includes(q));
   228     const matchFilter =
   229       filterBanned === 'all' ? true :
   230       filterBanned === 'banned' ? g.is_banned : !g.is_banned;
   231     return matchQ && matchFilter;
   232   });
   233 
   234   const filteredBans = bans.filter(b => {
   235     const q = search.toLowerCase();
   236     return !q ||
   237       (b.device_fp ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
   238       (b.device_id ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
   239       b.ban_reason.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
   240       (b.banned_by_name ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
   241       (b.associated_usernames ?? []).some(u => u.toLowerCase().includes(q));
   242   });
   243 
   244   const handleBan = async () => {
   245     if (!banTarget) return;
   246     setBanning(true);
   247     const res = await banDevice({
   248       device_fp:            banTarget.device_fp ?? undefined,
   249       device_id:            banTarget.device_id ?? undefined,
   250       hardware_hash:        banTarget.hardware_hash ?? undefined,
   251       ban_reason:           banNote.trim() || 'تعدد الحسابات على نفس الجهاز',
   252       ban_type:             'both',
   253       notes:                banNote.trim() || undefined,
   254       associated_user_ids:  banTarget.user_ids,
   255       associated_usernames: banTarget.usernames,
   256     });
   257     setBanning(false);
   258     if (res.success) {
   259       toast.success('✅ تم حظر الجهاز نهائياً');
   260       setBanTarget(null);
   261       setBanNote('');
   262       await load();
   263     } else {
   264       toast.error(res.error ?? 'فشل الحظر');
   265     }
   266   };
   267 
   268   const handleUnban = async () => {
   269     if (!unbanId) return;
   270     setUnbanning(true);
   271     const res = await unbanDevice(unbanId);
   272     setUnbanning(false);
   273     if (res.success) {
   274       toast.success('✅ تم رفع الحظر');
   275       setUnbanId(null);
   276       await load();
   277     } else {
   278       toast.error(res.error ?? 'فشل رفع الحظر');
   279     }
   280   };
   281 
   282   const activeBansCount = bans.filter(b => b.is_active).length;
   283 
   284   return (
   285     <AdminShell
   286       title="الحسابات المكررة وحظر الأجهزة"
   287       breadcrumbs={[
   288         { label: 'الإدارة', href: '/admin' },
   289         { label: 'الحسابات المكررة' },
   290       ]}
   291     >
   292       {/* إحصائيات سريعة */}
   293       <div className="grid grid-cols-3 gap-3 mb-4">
   294         {[
   295           { label: 'أجهزة مكررة', value: dupes.length, icon: Smartphone, color: 'text-warning' },
   296           { label: 'محظور منهم', value: dupes.filter(d => d.is_banned).length, icon: ShieldX, color: 'text-destructive' },
   297           { label: 'حظر نشط', value: activeBansCount, icon: Ban, color: 'text-destructive' },
   298         ].map(({ label, value, icon: Icon, color }) => (
   299           <div key={label} className="bg-card border border-border rounded-xl p-3 text-center">
   300             <Icon className={`w-5 h-5 mx-auto mb-1 ${color}`} />
   301             <p className="text-lg font-bold tabular-nums">{loading ? '—' : value}</p>
   302             <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">{label}</p>
   303           </div>
   304         ))}
   305       </div>
   306 
   307       {/* شريط البحث + تحديث */}
   308       <div className="flex gap-2 mb-4">
   309         <div className="relative flex-1">
   310           <Search className="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 w-3.5 h-3.5 text-muted-foreground" />


</observation>

   418                 placeholder="مثال: إنشاء حسابات متعددة للاستفادة من العروض"
   419                 value={banNote}
   420                 onChange={e => setBanNote(e.target.value)}
   421                 className="text-sm"
   422                 dir="rtl"
   423               />
   424             </div>
   425 
   426             <div className="flex gap-2">
   427               <Button
   428                 variant="destructive"
   429                 className="flex-1 gap-2"
   430                 onClick={handleBan}
   431                 disabled={banning}
   432               >
   433                 {banning ? <Loader2 className="w-4 h-4 animate-spin" /> : <Ban className="w-4 h-4" />}
   434                 تأكيد الحظر
   435               </Button>
   436               <Button variant="outline" className="flex-1" onClick={() => setBanTarget(null)} disabled={banning}>
   437                 إلغاء
   438               </Button>
   439             </div>
   440           </div>
   441         </div>
   442       )}
   443 
   444       {/* حوار تأكيد رفع الحظر */}
   445       <ConfirmDialog
   446         open={!!unbanId}
   447         onOpenChange={(v) => { if (!v) setUnbanId(null); }}
   448         title="رفع حظر الجهاز"
   449         description="هل تريد رفع الحظر عن هذا الجهاز؟ سيتمكن المستخدم من تسجيل الدخول مجدداً."
   450         variant="default"
   451         onConfirm={handleUnban}
   452       />
   453     </AdminShell>
   454   );
   455 }

```
// ── الحسابات المحظورة (is_active = false) ─────────────────────────────────
export interface BannedAccount {
  id: string;
  username: string | null;
  email: string | null;
  full_name: string | null;
  phone: string | null;
  role: string;
  device_fp: string | null;
  created_at: string;
  updated_at: string;
}

/** جلب جميع الحسابات المحظورة (is_active = false) */
export async function getBannedAccounts(): Promise<{ data: BannedAccount[]; error?: string }> {
  const { data, error } = await supabase
    .from('profiles')
    .select('id, username, email, full_name, phone, role, device_fp, created_at, updated_at')
    .eq('is_active', false)
    .order('updated_at', { ascending: false });
  if (error) return { data: [], error: error.message };
  return { data: (data ?? []) as BannedAccount[] };
}
```

```
// صفحة إدارة الحسابات المكررة وحظر الأجهزة — v3.0.249

function fmt(d?: string | null) {
  if (!d) return '—';
  try { return format(new Date(d), 'dd MMM yyyy HH:mm', { locale: ar }); }
  catch { return d; }
}
function fmtDate(d?: string | null) {
  if (!d) return '—';

  catch { return d; }
}
function shortFp(fp?: string | null) {
  if (!fp) return '—';
  return fp.length > 12 ? `${fp.slice(0, 6)}…${fp.slice(-6)}` : fp;
}

// ── بطاقة مجموعة جهاز مكرر ────────────────────────────────────────────────
function DuplicateGroupCard({
  group, onBan,
}: {
  group: DuplicateDeviceGroup;
  onBan: (g: DuplicateDeviceGroup) => void;
}) {
  const [expanded, setExpanded] = useState(false);
  return (
    <div className={`rounded-2xl border bg-card overflow-hidden transition-colors ${group.is_banned ? 'border-destructive/40' : 'border-border'}`}>
      <button
        className="w-full flex items-center gap-3 p-4 text-right"
        onClick={() => setExpanded(e => !e)}
      >
        <div className={`w-9 h-9 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 ${group.is_banned ? 'bg-destructive/10' : 'bg-warning/10'}`}>
          <Smartphone className={`w-4 h-4 ${group.is_banned ? 'text-destructive' : 'text-warning'}`} />
        </div>
        <div className="flex-1 min-w-0 text-right">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <p className="text-sm font-semibold truncate">{group.usernames.filter(Boolean).join('، ') || '—'}</p>
            {group.is_banned && <Badge variant="destructive" className="text-[9px] px-1.5 shrink-0">محظور</Badge>}
          </div>
          <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-0.5">
            {group.user_count} حسابات · بصمة: {shortFp(group.device_fp)}
          </p>
        </div>
        {expanded ? <ChevronUp className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" /> : <ChevronDown className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" />}
      </button>

      {expanded && (
        <div className="px-4 pb-4 space-y-3 border-t border-border pt-3">
          {/* الأرقام */}
          {group.phones.filter(Boolean).length > 0 && (
            <div className="flex items-start gap-2">
              <PhoneCall className="w-3.5 h-3.5 text-muted-foreground mt-0.5 shrink-0" />
              <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground break-all">{group.phones.filter(Boolean).join('، ')}</p>
            </div>
          )}
          {/* معرفات الجهاز */}
          {group.device_fp && (
            <div className="bg-muted/50 rounded-xl p-3 space-y-1.5 text-xs">
              <p className="text-muted-foreground"><span className="font-medium text-foreground">Device FP: </span>{group.device_fp}</p>
              {group.device_id && <p className="text-muted-foreground"><span className="font-medium text-foreground">Device ID: </span>{group.device_id}</p>}
              {group.hardware_hash && <p className="text-muted-foreground"><span className="font-medium text-foreground">HW Hash: </span>{shortFp(group.hardware_hash)}</p>}
            </div>
          )}
          {/* تواريخ */}
          <div className="flex gap-3 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
            <span>أول ظهور: {fmt(group.first_seen)}</span>
            <span>·</span>
            <span>آخر نشاط: {fmt(group.last_seen)}</span>
          </div>
          {/* معلومات الحظر */}
          {group.is_banned && group.ban_info && (
            <div className="bg-destructive/5 border border-destructive/15 rounded-xl p-3 text-xs space-y-1">
              <p className="font-medium text-destructive">سبب الحظر: {group.ban_info.ban_reason ?? '—'}</p>
              <p className="text-muted-foreground">بواسطة: {group.ban_info.banned_by_name ?? '—'} · {fmt(group.ban_info.banned_at)}</p>
            </div>
          )}
          {/* أزرار */}
          {!group.is_banned && (
            <Button
              variant="destructive" size="sm"
              className="w-full gap-2 mt-1"
              onClick={() => onBan(group)}
            >
              <Ban className="w-3.5 h-3.5" /> حظر الجهاز نهائياً
            </Button>
          )}
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// ── بطاقة حظر جهاز ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function BanCard({ ban, onUnban }: { ban: DeviceBan; onUnban: (id: string) => void }) {
  const [expanded, setExpanded] = useState(false);
  return (
    <div className={`rounded-2xl border bg-card overflow-hidden ${ban.is_active ? 'border-destructive/40' : 'border-border opacity-60'}`}>
      <button className="w-full flex items-center gap-3 p-4 text-right" onClick={() => setExpanded(e => !e)}>
        <div className={`w-9 h-9 rounded-xl flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 ${ban.is_active ? 'bg-destructive/10' : 'bg-muted'}`}>
          {ban.is_active ? <ShieldX className="w-4 h-4 text-destructive" /> : <ShieldCheck className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground" />}
        </div>
        <div className="flex-1 min-w-0 text-right">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2">
            <p className="text-sm font-semibold truncate">{(ban.associated_usernames ?? []).join('، ') || shortFp(ban.device_fp)}</p>
            <Badge variant={ban.is_active ? 'destructive' : 'secondary'} className="text-[9px] px-1.5 shrink-0">
              {ban.is_active ? 'نشط' : 'مرفوع'}
            </Badge>
          </div>
          <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-0.5">{ban.ban_reason} · {fmt(ban.banned_at)}</p>
        </div>
        {expanded ? <ChevronUp className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" /> : <ChevronDown className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" />}
      </button>
      {expanded && (
        <div className="px-4 pb-4 border-t border-border pt-3 space-y-3">
          <div className="bg-muted/50 rounded-xl p-3 space-y-1.5 text-xs">
            {ban.device_fp    && <p className="text-muted-foreground"><span className="font-medium text-foreground">Device FP: </span>{ban.device_fp}</p>}
            {ban.device_id    && <p className="text-muted-foreground"><span className="font-medium text-foreground">Device ID: </span>{ban.device_id}</p>}
            {ban.hardware_hash && <p className="text-muted-foreground"><span className="font-medium text-foreground">HW Hash: </span>{shortFp(ban.hardware_hash)}</p>}
            {ban.platform      && <p className="text-muted-foreground"><span className="font-medium text-foreground">Platform: </span>{ban.platform}</p>}
          </div>
          <div className="text-xs text-muted-foreground space-y-1">
            <p>بواسطة: {ban.banned_by_name ?? '—'}</p>
            {ban.notes && <p>ملاحظات: {ban.notes}</p>}
            {ban.unbanned_at && <p>رُفع في: {fmt(ban.unbanned_at)}</p>}
          </div>
          {ban.is_active && (
            <Button variant="outline" size="sm" className="w-full gap-2 mt-1 text-destructive border-destructive/40 hover:bg-destructive/5"
              onClick={() => onUnban(ban.id)}>
              <ShieldCheck className="w-3.5 h-3.5" /> رفع الحظر
            </Button>
          )}
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// ── بطاقة حساب محظور ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────
function BannedAccountCard({
  account, onRestore,
}: {
  account: BannedAccount;
  onRestore: (id: string, username: string | null) => void;
}) {
  const [expanded, setExpanded] = useState(false);
  return (
    <div className="rounded-2xl border border-destructive/30 bg-card overflow-hidden">
      <button className="w-full flex items-center gap-3 p-4 text-right" onClick={() => setExpanded(e => !e)}>
        <div className="w-9 h-9 rounded-xl bg-destructive/10 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">
          <UserX className="w-4 h-4 text-destructive" />
        </div>
        <div className="flex-1 min-w-0 text-right">
          <p className="text-sm font-semibold truncate">{account.username ?? account.email ?? account.id}</p>
          <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground mt-0.5">{account.phone ?? '—'} · {account.role}</p>
        </div>
        {expanded ? <ChevronUp className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" /> : <ChevronDown className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" />}
      </button>
      {expanded && (
        <div className="px-4 pb-4 border-t border-border pt-3 space-y-3">
          <div className="bg-muted/50 rounded-xl p-3 space-y-1.5 text-xs">
            {account.email && <p className="text-muted-foreground"><span className="font-medium text-foreground">البريد: </span>{account.email}</p>}
            {account.full_name && <p className="text-muted-foreground"><span className="font-medium text-foreground">الاسم: </span>{account.full_name}</p>}
            {account.device_fp && <p className="text-muted-foreground"><span className="font-medium text-foreground">Device FP: </span>{shortFp(account.device_fp)}</p>}
          </div>
          <div className="flex gap-3 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
            <span className="flex items-center gap-1"><Calendar className="w-3 h-3" />{fmtDate(account.created_at)}</span>
            <span>·</span>
            <span className="flex items-center gap-1"><Hash className="w-3 h-3" />{account.id.slice(0, 8)}</span>
          </div>
          <Button variant="outline" size="sm" className="w-full gap-2 mt-1 text-green-600 border-green-600/40 hover:bg-green-50"
            onClick={() => onRestore(account.id, account.username)}>
            <CheckCircle className="w-3.5 h-3.5" /> رفع الحظر وتفعيل الحساب
          </Button>
        </div>
      )}
    </div>
  );
}

// ── الصفحة الرئيسية ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
export default function AdminDuplicateAccounts() {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const [tab, setTab] = useState<'duplicates' | 'banned_accounts' | 'bans'>('duplicates');

  const [dupes,          setDupes]          = useState<DuplicateDeviceGroup[]>([]);
  const [bans,           setBans]           = useState<DeviceBan[]>([]);
  const [bannedAccounts, setBannedAccounts] = useState<BannedAccount[]>([]);
  const [loading,        setLoading]        = useState(true);
  const [scanning,       setScanning]       = useState(false);
  const [search,         setSearch]         = useState('');
  const [filterBanned,   setFilterBanned]   = useState<'all' | 'banned' | 'unbanned'>('all');

  // حوار حظر جهاز
  const [banTarget, setBanTarget] = useState<DuplicateDeviceGroup | null>(null);
  const [banNote,   setBanNote]   = useState('');
  const [banning,   setBanning]   = useState(false);

  // حوار رفع حظر جهاز
  const [unbanId,    setUnbanId]   = useState<string | null>(null);
  const [unbanning,  setUnbanning] = useState(false);

  // حوار تفعيل حساب محظور
  const [restoreTarget, setRestoreTarget] = useState<{ id: string; name: string | null } | null>(null);
  const [restoring,     setRestoring]     = useState(false);

  // ── جلب البيانات ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const load = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      const [d, b, ba] = await Promise.all([
        getDuplicateDevices(),
        getDeviceBans(),
        getBannedAccounts(),
      ]);
      if (d.success) setDupes(d.data);
      else toast.error(d.error ?? 'فشل جلب الأجهزة المكررة');
      if (b.success) setBans(b.data);
      setBannedAccounts(ba.data);
    } finally { setLoading(false); }
  }, []);

  // ── فحص شامل ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const handleScan = useCallback(async () => {
    setScanning(true);
    toast.info('🔍 جاري الفحص الشامل…');
    try {
      const [d, b, ba] = await Promise.all([
        getDuplicateDevices(),
        getDeviceBans(),
        getBannedAccounts(),
      ]);
      if (d.success) {
        setDupes(d.data);
        toast.success(`✅ تم — ${d.data.length} جهاز مكرر · ${d.data.filter(x => x.is_banned).length} محظور`);
      } else toast.error(d.error ?? 'فشل الفحص');
      if (b.success) setBans(b.data);
      setBannedAccounts(ba.data);
      if (ba.data.length > 0) toast.info(`⚠️ ${ba.data.length} حساب محظور في قاعدة البيانات`);
    } finally { setScanning(false); }
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => { load(); }, [load]);

  // ── تصفية ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const filteredDupes = dupes.filter(g => {
    const q = search.toLowerCase();
    const matchQ = !q ||
      (g.device_fp ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
      (g.device_id ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
      g.usernames.some(u => (u ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q)) ||
      g.phones.some(p => (p ?? '').includes(q));
    const matchFilter =
      filterBanned === 'all' ? true :
      filterBanned === 'banned' ? g.is_banned : !g.is_banned;
    return matchQ && matchFilter;
  });

  const filteredBans = bans.filter(b => {
    const q = search.toLowerCase();
    return !q ||
      (b.device_fp ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
      (b.device_id ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
      b.ban_reason.toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
      (b.banned_by_name ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
      (b.associated_usernames ?? []).some(u => u.toLowerCase().includes(q));
  });

  const filteredBannedAccounts = bannedAccounts.filter(a => {
    const q = search.toLowerCase();
    return !q ||
      (a.username ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
      (a.email ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) ||
      (a.phone ?? '').includes(q) ||
      (a.full_name ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q);
  });

  // ── حظر جهاز ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const handleBan = async () => {
    if (!banTarget) return;
    setBanning(true);
    const res = await banDevice({
      device_fp:            banTarget.device_fp ?? undefined,
      device_id:            banTarget.device_id ?? undefined,
      hardware_hash:        banTarget.hardware_hash ?? undefined,
      ban_reason:           banNote.trim() || 'تعدد الحسابات على نفس الجهاز',
      ban_type:             'both',
      notes:                banNote.trim() || undefined,
      associated_user_ids:  banTarget.user_ids,
      associated_usernames: banTarget.usernames,
    });
    setBanning(false);
    if (res.success) {
      toast.success('✅ تم حظر الجهاز نهائياً');
      setBanTarget(null);
      setBanNote('');
      await load();
    } else toast.error(res.error ?? 'فشل الحظر');
  };

  // ── رفع حظر جهاز ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const handleUnban = async () => {
    if (!unbanId) return;
    setUnbanning(true);
    const res = await unbanDevice(unbanId);
    setUnbanning(false);
    if (res.success) {
      toast.success('✅ تم رفع الحظر');
      setUnbanId(null);
      await load();
    } else toast.error(res.error ?? 'فشل رفع الحظر');
  };

  // ── تفعيل حساب محظور ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  const handleRestore = async () => {
    if (!restoreTarget) return;
    setRestoring(true);
    const { error } = await toggleUserActive(restoreTarget.id, true);
    setRestoring(false);
    if (!error) {
      toast.success(`✅ تم تفعيل الحساب: ${restoreTarget.name ?? restoreTarget.id}`);
      setRestoreTarget(null);
      await load();
    } else toast.error(typeof error === 'string' ? error : 'فشل التفعيل');
  };

  const activeBansCount = bans.filter(b => b.is_active).length;

  return (
    <AdminShell
      title="الحسابات المكررة وحظر الأجهزة"
      breadcrumbs={[
        { label: 'الإدارة', href: '/admin' },
        { label: 'الحسابات المكررة' },
      ]}
      actions={
        <Button variant="outline" size="sm" onClick={handleScan} disabled={scanning} className="gap-1.5 h-8">
          {scanning ? <Loader2 className="w-3.5 h-3.5 animate-spin" /> : <ScanSearch className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />}
          فحص شامل
        </Button>
      }
    >
      {/* إحصائيات سريعة */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-4 gap-2 mb-4">
        {[
          { label: 'أجهزة مكررة',     value: dupes.length,                            icon: Smartphone, color: 'text-warning' },
          { label: 'محظور الأجهزة',   value: dupes.filter(d => d.is_banned).length,    icon: ShieldX,    color: 'text-destructive' },
          { label: 'حسابات محظورة',   value: bannedAccounts.length,                    icon: UserX,      color: 'text-destructive' },
          { label: 'حظر جهاز نشط',    value: activeBansCount,                          icon: Ban,        color: 'text-destructive' },
        ].map(({ label, value, icon: Icon, color }) => (
          <div key={label} className="bg-card border border-border rounded-xl p-2.5 text-center">
            <Icon className={`w-4 h-4 mx-auto mb-1 ${color}`} />
            <p className="text-base font-bold tabular-nums">{loading ? '—' : value}</p>
            <p className="text-[9px] text-muted-foreground leading-tight">{label}</p>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* شريط البحث + تحديث */}
      <div className="flex gap-2 mb-4">
        <div className="relative flex-1">
          <Search className="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 w-3.5 h-3.5 text-muted-foreground" />
          <Input
            placeholder="ابحث بالاسم أو الجهاز أو الهاتف…"
            value={search}
            onChange={e => setSearch(e.target.value)}
            className="pr-9 text-sm h-9"
            dir="rtl"
          />
        </div>
        <Button variant="outline" size="sm" onClick={load} disabled={loading} className="shrink-0 h-9 w-9 p-0">
          {loading ? <Loader2 className="w-4 h-4 animate-spin" /> : <RefreshCw className="w-4 h-4" />}
        </Button>
      </div>

      <Tabs value={tab} onValueChange={v => setTab(v as typeof tab)}>
        <TabsList className="w-full mb-4 h-auto">
          {/* تبويب 1: أجهزة مكررة */}
          <TabsTrigger value="duplicates" className="flex-1 gap-1 text-xs py-2 flex-col sm:flex-row">
            <AlertTriangle className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
            <span>أجهزة مكررة</span>
            {dupes.length > 0 && (
              <Badge variant="secondary" className="text-[9px] px-1.5 py-0">{dupes.length}</Badge>
            )}
          </TabsTrigger>
          {/* تبويب 2: الحسابات المحظورة */}
          <TabsTrigger value="banned_accounts" className="flex-1 gap-1 text-xs py-2 flex-col sm:flex-row">
            <UserX className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
            <span>حسابات محظورة</span>
            {bannedAccounts.length > 0 && (
              <Badge variant="destructive" className="text-[9px] px-1.5 py-0">{bannedAccounts.length}</Badge>
            )}
          </TabsTrigger>
          {/* تبويب 3: قائمة الحظر */}
          <TabsTrigger value="bans" className="flex-1 gap-1 text-xs py-2 flex-col sm:flex-row">
            <ShieldX className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />
            <span>حظر الأجهزة</span>
            {activeBansCount > 0 && (
              <Badge variant="destructive" className="text-[9px] px-1.5 py-0">{activeBansCount}</Badge>
            )}
          </TabsTrigger>
        </TabsList>

        {/* ── تبويب الأجهزة المكررة ── */}
        <TabsContent value="duplicates" className="space-y-3 mt-0">
          <div className="flex gap-2 flex-wrap">
            {([['all', 'الكل'], ['unbanned', 'غير محظور'], ['banned', 'محظور']] as const).map(([v, l]) => (
              <button key={v}
                onClick={() => setFilterBanned(v)}
                className={`text-xs px-3 py-1.5 rounded-full border transition-colors ${filterBanned === v ? 'bg-primary text-primary-foreground border-primary' : 'bg-card border-border text-muted-foreground'}`}
              >{l}</button>
            ))}
          </div>
          {loading ? (
            <div className="flex items-center justify-center py-12">
              <Loader2 className="w-6 h-6 animate-spin text-muted-foreground" />
            </div>
          ) : filteredDupes.length === 0 ? (
            <div className="text-center py-12 text-muted-foreground">
              <CheckCircle className="w-10 h-10 mx-auto mb-3 text-green-500/60" />
              <p className="text-sm font-medium">لا توجد أجهزة مكررة</p>
              <p className="text-xs mt-1">اضغط "فحص شامل" للتحقق من قاعدة البيانات</p>
            </div>
          ) : (
            filteredDupes.map((g, i) => (
              <DuplicateGroupCard
                key={g.device_fp ?? g.device_id ?? i}
                group={g}
                onBan={setBanTarget}
              />
            ))
          )}
        </TabsContent>

        {/* ── تبويب الحسابات المحظورة ── */}
        <TabsContent value="banned_accounts" className="space-y-3 mt-0">
          {loading ? (
            <div className="flex items-center justify-center py-12">
              <Loader2 className="w-6 h-6 animate-spin text-muted-foreground" />
            </div>
          ) : filteredBannedAccounts.length === 0 ? (
            <div className="text-center py-12 text-muted-foreground">
              <Users className="w-10 h-10 mx-auto mb-3 text-green-500/60" />
              <p className="text-sm font-medium">لا توجد حسابات محظورة</p>
              <p className="text-xs mt-1">جميع الحسابات نشطة</p>
            </div>
          ) : (
            filteredBannedAccounts.map(a => (
              <BannedAccountCard
                key={a.id}
                account={a}
                onRestore={(id, name) => setRestoreTarget({ id, name })}
              />
            ))
          )}
        </TabsContent>

        {/* ── تبويب قائمة حظر الأجهزة ── */}
        <TabsContent value="bans" className="space-y-3 mt-0">
          {loading ? (
            <div className="flex items-center justify-center py-12">
              <Loader2 className="w-6 h-6 animate-spin text-muted-foreground" />
            </div>
          ) : filteredBans.length === 0 ? (
            <div className="text-center py-12 text-muted-foreground">
              <ShieldCheck className="w-10 h-10 mx-auto mb-3 text-green-500/60" />
              <p className="text-sm font-medium">قائمة الحظر فارغة</p>
              <p className="text-xs mt-1">لم يتم حظر أي جهاز بعد</p>
            </div>
          ) : (
            filteredBans.map(b => (
              <BanCard key={b.id} ban={b} onUnban={setUnbanId} />
            ))
          )}
        </TabsContent>
      </Tabs>

      {/* حوار تأكيد حظر جهاز */}
      {banTarget && (
        <div className="fixed inset-0 bg-black/60 z-50 flex items-end md:items-center justify-center p-4" dir="rtl">
          <div className="bg-card border border-border rounded-2xl w-full max-w-sm p-5 space-y-4">
            <div className="flex items-center gap-3">
              <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-xl bg-destructive/10 flex items-center justify-center">
                <Ban className="w-5 h-5 text-destructive" />
              </div>
              <div>
                <h3 className="font-bold text-sm">حظر الجهاز نهائياً</h3>
                <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">
                  {banTarget.user_count} حسابات · {shortFp(banTarget.device_fp)}
                </p>
              </div>
            </div>
            <div className="bg-destructive/5 border border-destructive/15 rounded-xl p-3 text-xs text-muted-foreground leading-relaxed">
              ⚠️ سيُمنع الجهاز من الدخول حتى لو حذف التطبيق أو مسح البيانات أو أعاد التثبيت.
            </div>
            <div>
              <p className="text-xs font-medium mb-1.5">سبب الحظر (اختياري)</p>
              <Input
                placeholder="مثال: إنشاء حسابات متعددة للاستفادة من العروض"
                value={banNote}
                onChange={e => setBanNote(e.target.value)}
                className="text-sm"
                dir="rtl"
              />
            </div>
            <div className="flex gap-2">
              <Button variant="destructive" className="flex-1 gap-2" onClick={handleBan} disabled={banning}>
                {banning ? <Loader2 className="w-4 h-4 animate-spin" /> : <Ban className="w-4 h-4" />}
                تأكيد الحظر
              </Button>
              <Button variant="outline" className="flex-1" onClick={() => setBanTarget(null)} disabled={banning}>
                إلغاء
              </Button>
            </div>
          </div>
        </div>
      )}

      {/* حوار رفع حظر جهاز */}
      <ConfirmDialog
        open={!!unbanId}
        onOpenChange={v => { if (!v) setUnbanId(null); }}
        title="رفع حظر الجهاز"
        description="هل تريد رفع الحظر عن هذا الجهاز؟ سيتمكن المستخدم من تسجيل الدخول مجدداً."
        variant="default"
        onConfirm={handleUnban}
      />

      {/* حوار تفعيل حساب محظور */}
      <ConfirmDialog
        open={!!restoreTarget}
        onOpenChange={v => { if (!v) setRestoreTarget(null); }}
        title="تفعيل الحساب"
        description={`هل تريد رفع الحظر وتفعيل حساب "${restoreTarget?.name ?? restoreTarget?.id}"؟`}
        confirmLabel={restoring ? 'جاري التفعيل…' : 'تفعيل'}
        variant="default"
        onConfirm={handleRestore}
      />
    </AdminShell>
  );
}
```

// ── بطاقة مجموعة أجهزة مكررة ─────────────────────────────────────────────
function DuplicateGroupCard({
  group, onBan,
}: { group: DuplicateDeviceGroup; onBan: (g: DuplicateDeviceGroup) => void }) {
  const [expanded, setExpanded] = useState(false);
  return (
    <div className={`rounded-xl border bg-card transition-all ${group.is_banned ? 'border-destructive/30 bg-destructive/3' : 'border-border'}`}>
      {/* رأس البطاقة */}
      <button
        className="w-full flex items-center gap-3 p-4 text-right"
        onClick={() => setExpanded(v => !v)}
      >
        <div className={`w-10 h-10 rounded-lg flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 ${group.is_banned ? 'bg-destructive/10 text-destructive' : 'bg-warning/10 text-warning'}`}>
          {group.is_banned ? <ShieldX className="w-5 h-5" /> : <AlertTriangle className="w-5 h-5" />}
        </div>
        <div className="flex-1 min-w-0 text-right">
          <div className="flex items-center gap-2 flex-wrap">
            <span className="text-sm font-semibold">
              {group.user_count} حسابات على نفس الجهاز
            </span>
            {group.is_banned && (
              <Badge variant="destructive" className="text-[10px]">محظور</Badge>
            )}
          </div>
          <p className="text-[11px] text-muted-foreground font-mono mt-0.5 truncate">
            FP: {shortFp(group.device_fp)}
            {group.device_id ? ` · ID: ${shortFp(group.device_id)}` : ''}
          </p>
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 shrink-0">
          <span className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">{fmt(group.last_seen)}</span>
          {expanded ? <ChevronUp className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground" /> : <ChevronDown className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground" />}
        </div>
      </button>

      {/* تفاصيل موسّعة */}
      {expanded && (
        <div className="border-t border-border px-4 pb-4 pt-3 space-y-3">
          {/* معرفات الجهاز */}
          <div className="bg-muted/40 rounded-lg p-3 space-y-1.5 text-xs font-mono">
            {group.device_fp && (
              <p className="break-all"><span className="text-muted-foreground">device_fp: </span>{group.device_fp}</p>
            )}
            {group.device_id && (
              <p className="break-all"><span className="text-muted-foreground">device_id: </span>{group.device_id}</p>
            )}
            {group.hardware_hash && (
              <p className="break-all"><span className="text-muted-foreground">hw_hash: </span>{group.hardware_hash}</p>
            )}
          </div>

          {/* الحسابات المرتبطة */}
          <div>
            <p className="text-xs font-semibold text-muted-foreground mb-2 flex items-center gap-1">
              <Users className="w-3 h-3" /> الحسابات المرتبطة ({group.user_count})
            </p>
            <div className="space-y-1.5">
              {group.usernames.map((name, i) => (
                <div key={i} className="flex items-center justify-between bg-muted/30 rounded-lg px-3 py-2">
                  <span className="text-xs font-mono text-muted-foreground">{group.user_ids[i]?.slice(0, 8)}…</span>
                  <div className="text-right">
                    <p className="text-xs font-semibold">{name ?? '—'}</p>
                    <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">{group.phones?.[i] ?? '—'}</p>
                  </div>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          </div>

          {/* معلومات الحظر الحالية */}
          {group.is_banned && group.ban_info && (
            <div className="bg-destructive/5 border border-destructive/20 rounded-lg p-3">
              <p className="text-xs font-semibold text-destructive mb-1">معلومات الحظر</p>
              <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">السبب: {group.ban_info.ban_reason ?? '—'}</p>
              <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground">بواسطة: {group.ban_info.banned_by_name ?? '—'}</p>

          APK_PATH=$(find android/app/build/outputs/apk/release -name "*.apk" | head -1)
          if [[ -z "$APK_PATH" ]]; then
            echo "❌ No APK found after build!"
          cp "$APK_PATH" "${{ env.APK_NAME }}"

--BEGIN AGENT OBSERVATION--
name: Build Vodafone Fakka APK

on:
  push:
    branches: [main, master]
  workflow_dispatch:

env:
  SUPABASE_URL: https://vchmsnavyhripakyvzom.supabase.co

# ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════
#  Atomic Deployment Pipeline — الترتيب الصحيح الوحيد المسموح به:
#
#  1. Build  ➜  2. Sign  ➜  3. Upload  ➜  4. Verify HTTP 200  ➜
#  5. Download Test  ➜  6. Update DB  ➜  7. Send Notification  ➜
#  8. Force Update
#
#  ممنوع: أي خطوة تعتمد على خطوة لم تنجح بعد.
#  أي فشل في (1–5) = إلغاء النشر كاملاً بدون تحديث DB أو إشعار.
# ═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════

jobs:
  build:
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    timeout-minutes: 45
    steps:
      - uses: actions/checkout@v4

      # ─── [0] استخراج الإصدار أولاً — قبل أي شيء ──────────────────────────
      - name: Read version from build.gradle
        id: version
        run: |
          APP_VERSION=$(grep 'versionName' android/app/build.gradle | head -1 \
            | sed 's/.*versionName "\(.*\)".*/\1/' | tr -d '[:space:]')
          APP_VERSION_CODE=$(grep 'versionCode' android/app/build.gradle | head -1 \
            | sed 's/.*versionCode \([0-9]*\).*/\1/' | tr -d '[:space:]')
          APK_NAME="VodafoneFakka-v${APP_VERSION}.apk"
          APK_PUBLIC_URL="${{ env.SUPABASE_URL }}/storage/v1/object/public/apk-releases/${APK_NAME}"
          echo "APP_VERSION=$APP_VERSION"           >> $GITHUB_ENV
          echo "APP_VERSION_CODE=$APP_VERSION_CODE" >> $GITHUB_ENV
          echo "APK_NAME=$APK_NAME"                 >> $GITHUB_ENV
          echo "APK_PUBLIC_URL=$APK_PUBLIC_URL"     >> $GITHUB_ENV
          echo "✅ Version: $APP_VERSION (code $APP_VERSION_CODE) → $APK_NAME"

      - name: Setup pnpm
        uses: pnpm/action-setup@v2
        with:
          version: 10

      - name: Setup Node.js
        uses: actions/setup-node@v4
        with:
          node-version: 24
          cache: 'pnpm'

      # ─── [1] BUILD ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
      - name: Install dependencies & build Vite
        run: |
          pnpm install --frozen-lockfile
          npx vite build --minify true --outDir dist
          echo "✅ Vite build OK"

      - name: Setup JDK 17
        uses: actions/setup-java@v4
        with:
          distribution: 'temurin'
          java-version: '17'

      - name: Setup Android SDK
        uses: android-actions/setup-android@v3

      - name: Fix local.properties SDK path
        run: echo "sdk.dir=$ANDROID_SDK_ROOT" > android/local.properties

      - name: Capacitor sync
        run: pnpm exec cap sync android

      - name: Fix gradlew permissions
        run: chmod +x android/gradlew

      - name: Fix HTTP plugin namespace
        run: |
          HTTP_GRADLE=$(find node_modules -path "*capacitor-community/http*/android/build.gradle" | head -1)
          if [[ -n "$HTTP_GRADLE" && $(grep -c "namespace" "$HTTP_GRADLE") -eq 0 ]]; then
            sed -i "s|android {|android {\n    namespace 'com.getcapacitor.community.http'|" "$HTTP_GRADLE"
          fi
          HTTP_MANIFEST=$(find node_modules -path "*capacitor-community/http*/android/src/main/AndroidManifest.xml" | head -1)
          [[ -n "$HTTP_MANIFEST" ]] && sed -i 's/ package="[^"]*"//' "$HTTP_MANIFEST" || true

      # ─── [2] SIGN ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
      - name: Build signed APK
        run: |
          cd android && ./gradlew assembleRelease --no-daemon
          echo "✅ Gradle build + sign OK"
        env:
          KEYSTORE_PASSWORD: vodafone123
          KEY_ALIAS: vfkey

      # ─── [3] PREPARE APK ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
      - name: Rename APK + compute hash
        run: |
          APK_PATH=$(find android/app/build/outputs/apk/release -name "*.apk" | head -1)
          if [[ -z "$APK_PATH" ]]; then
            echo "❌ No APK found after build!"
            exit 1
          fi
          cp "$APK_PATH" "${{ env.APK_NAME }}"
          APK_HASH=$(md5sum "${{ env.APK_NAME }}" | awk '{print $1}')
          APK_SIZE=$(stat -c%s "${{ env.APK_NAME }}")
          echo "APK_HASH=$APK_HASH" >> $GITHUB_ENV
          echo "APK_SIZE=$APK_SIZE" >> $GITHUB_ENV
          echo "✅ APK ready: ${{ env.APK_NAME }} | size=${APK_SIZE} bytes | md5=$APK_HASH"

      - name: Upload APK artifact
        uses: actions/upload-artifact@v4
        with:
          name: VodafoneFakka-v${{ env.APP_VERSION }}
          path: ${{ env.APK_NAME }}

      # ─── [4] UPLOAD ────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
      - name: Upload APK to Supabase Storage
        env:
          SB_SERVICE_KEY: eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJzdXBhYmFzZSIsInJlZiI6InZjaG1zbmF2eWhyaXBha3l2em9tIiwicm9sZSI6InNlcnZpY2Vfcm9sZSIsImlhdCI6MTc4MjI4Nzg1NSwiZXhwIjoyMDk3ODYzODU1fQ.qGv6iURGQONn7wlG55S8HMCxTfodI2GQfcV4PkpARIo
        run: |
          echo "📤 Uploading ${{ env.APK_NAME }} to Supabase Storage..."
          UPLOAD_HTTP=$(curl -s -o /tmp/upload_response.txt -w "%{http_code}" -X POST \
            "${{ env.SUPABASE_URL }}/storage/v1/object/apk-releases/${{ env.APK_NAME }}" \
            -H "Authorization: Bearer $SB_SERVICE_KEY" \
            -H "apikey: $SB_SERVICE_KEY" \
            -H "Content-Type: application/vnd.android.package-archive" \
            -H "x-upsert: true" \
            --data-binary "@${{ env.APK_NAME }}")
          echo "Upload HTTP status: $UPLOAD_HTTP"
          cat /tmp/upload_response.txt
          if [[ "$UPLOAD_HTTP" != "200" ]]; then
            echo "❌ UPLOAD FAILED — aborting deployment. No DB update, no notification."
            exit 1
          fi
          echo "✅ Upload successful"

      # ─── [5a] VERIFY: URL returns HTTP 200 ────────────────────────────────
      - name: Verify APK URL returns HTTP 200
        env:
          SB_SERVICE_KEY: eyJhbGciOiJIUzI1NiIsInR5cCI6IkpXVCJ9.eyJpc3MiOiJzdXBhYmFzZSIsInJlZiI6InZjaG1zbmF2eWhyaXBha3l2em9tIiwicm9sZSI6InNlcnZpY2Vfcm9sZSIsImlhdCI6MTc4MjI4Nzg1NSwiZXhwIjoyMDk3ODYzODU1fQ.qGv6iURGQONn7wlG55S8HMCxTfodI2GQfcV4PkpARIo
        run: |
          echo "🔍 Verifying APK URL: ${{ env.APK_PUBLIC_URL }}"
          # انتظر 5 ثوانٍ لضمان CDN propagation
          sleep 5

          # محاولة حتى 5 مرات بفاصل 10 ثوانٍ
          for i in 1 2 3 4 5; do
            VERIFY_HTTP=$(curl -s -o /dev/null -w "%{http_code}" \
              -H "Authorization: Bearer $SB_SERVICE_KEY" \
              -H "apikey: $SB_SERVICE_KEY" \
              "${{ env.APK_PUBLIC_URL }}")
            echo "Attempt $i: HTTP $VERIFY_HTTP"
            if [[ "$VERIFY_HTTP" == "200" ]]; then
              echo "✅ URL verified — returns HTTP 200"
              break
            fi
            if [[ $i -eq 5 ]]; then
              echo "❌ URL NOT ACCESSIBLE after 5 attempts (last: HTTP $VERIFY_HTTP)"
              echo "❌ Aborting — No DB update, no notification sent."
              exit 1
            fi
            echo "⏳ Waiting 10s before retry..."
            sleep 10
          done

        run: |
          echo "📥 Partial download test (first 512KB)..."
          DL_HTTP=$(curl -s -o /tmp/apk_test.bin -w "%{http_code}" \
            -H "Authorization: Bearer $SB_SERVICE_KEY" \
            -H "apikey: $SB_SERVICE_KEY" \
            -H "Range: bytes=0-524287" \
            "${{ env.APK_PUBLIC_URL }}")
          DL_SIZE=$(stat -c%s /tmp/apk_test.bin 2>/dev/null || echo 0)

          # HTTP 200 أو 206 كلاهما مقبول مع Range header

            echo "❌ Aborting — No DB update, no notification sent."
            exit 1

            -H "apikey: $SB_SERVICE_KEY" \
            -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
            -d "{\"is_latest\":false}"

          # تحديث app_config
          for KEY in version_latest_name version_latest_code version_apk_url; do
            if [ "$KEY" = "version_latest_name" ]; then VAL="${{ env.APP_VERSION }}"; fi
            if [ "$KEY" = "version_latest_code" ]; then VAL="${{ env.APP_VERSION_CODE }}"; fi
            if [ "$KEY" = "version_apk_url" ];     then VAL="${{ env.APK_PUBLIC_URL }}"; fi
            curl -s -X PATCH "${{ env.SUPABASE_URL }}/rest/v1/app_config?key=eq.$KEY" \
              -H "Authorization: Bearer $SB_SERVICE_KEY" \
              -H "apikey: $SB_SERVICE_KEY" \
              -H "Content-Type: application/json" \
              -d "{\"value\":\"$VAL\"}"
          done

```
/**
 * ForceUpdateScreen — شاشة التحديث الإجباري Full Screen
 * ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 * - تظهر عندما installedCode < min_version_code في DB
 * - لا يوجد زر تخطي أو إغلاق
 * - تمنع زر الرجوع على Android
 * - تفتح صفحة التحديث في Chrome Custom Tab (Browser.open)
 */
import { useEffect } from 'react';
import { Download, AlertTriangle } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { App as CapacitorApp } from '@capacitor/app';
import { Browser } from '@capacitor/browser';
import { Capacitor } from '@capacitor/core';

interface ForceUpdateScreenProps {
  apkUrl?: string;
  latestVersion?: string;
}

export default function ForceUpdateScreen({ apkUrl, latestVersion }: ForceUpdateScreenProps) {

  // منع زر الرجوع على Android — المستخدم لا يستطيع الهروب من الشاشة
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!Capacitor.isNativePlatform()) return;
    let handle: { remove: () => void } | null = null;
    CapacitorApp.addListener('backButton', () => {
      // لا تفعل شيئاً — ابقَ في شاشة التحديث
    }).then(h => { handle = h; });
    return () => { handle?.remove(); };
  }, []);

  const handleUpdate = async () => {
    // فتح رابط APK مباشرة في Browser.open → Chrome Custom Tab على Android
    // GitHub Releases يضمن تنزيل مباشر بدون مشاكل Content-Type
    const GH_APK = 'https://github.com/Nader77700/vodafone-fakka/releases/download/v3.0.235/VodafoneFakka-v3.0.235.apk';
    const SUPABASE_APK = 'https://vchmsnavyhripakyvzom.supabase.co/storage/v1/object/public/apk-releases/VodafoneFakka-v3.0.235.apk';
    // استخدام GitHub Release كمصدر أساسي — Supabase كـ fallback
    const downloadUrl = apkUrl?.includes('github.com') ? apkUrl : GH_APK;

    if (Capacitor.isNativePlatform()) {
      await Browser.open({ url: downloadUrl, windowName: '_system' });
    } else {
      window.open(downloadUrl, '_blank');
    }
  };
```
New String: ```
/**
 * ForceUpdateScreen — شاشة التحديث الإجباري Full Screen
 * ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
 * - تظهر عندما installedCode < min_version_code في DB
 * - لا يوجد زر تخطي أو إغلاق
 * - تمنع زر الرجوع على Android
 * - تفتح رابط APK من Supabase Storage مباشرة (NEVER GitHub)
 *
 * ⚠️ لا تستخدم روابط GitHub Releases هنا أبداً:
 *    - GitHub لا يحدّث latest release تلقائياً
 *    - سيحمّل المستخدم نسخة قديمة وتفشل الثبيت
 *    - الرابط الصحيح دائماً من DB → apkUrl من جدول app_versions
 */
import { useEffect } from 'react';
import { Download, AlertTriangle } from 'lucide-react';
import { Button } from '@/components/ui/button';
import { App as CapacitorApp } from '@capacitor/app';
import { Browser } from '@capacitor/browser';
import { Capacitor } from '@capacitor/core';

const SUPABASE_STORAGE = 'https://vchmsnavyhripakyvzom.supabase.co/storage/v1/object/public/apk-releases';

interface ForceUpdateScreenProps {
  apkUrl?: string;
  latestVersion?: string;
}

export default function ForceUpdateScreen({ apkUrl, latestVersion }: ForceUpdateScreenProps) {

  // منع زر الرجوع على Android — المستخدم لا يستطيع الهروب من الشاشة
  useEffect(() => {
    if (!Capacitor.isNativePlatform()) return;
    let handle: { remove: () => void } | null = null;
    CapacitorApp.addListener('backButton', () => {
      // لا تفعل شيئاً — ابقَ في شاشة التحديث
    }).then(h => { handle = h; });
    return () => { handle?.remove(); };
  }, []);

  const handleUpdate = async () => {
    // ── بناء رابط التنزيل بالأولوية: ─────────────────────────────────────
    // 1. apkUrl من DB (app_versions.apk_url) — المصدر الوحيد الصحيح
    // 2. بناء رابط Supabase من رقم الإصدار كـ fallback
    // ⛔ لا GitHub Releases أبداً — يبقى قديماً ولا يُحدَّث تلقائياً
    let downloadUrl: string;

    if (apkUrl && apkUrl.startsWith('https://') && apkUrl.includes('apk-releases')) {
      // الرابط من DB صحيح ومن Supabase Storage ✅
      downloadUrl = apkUrl;
    } else if (latestVersion) {
      // بناء الرابط من رقم الإصدار كـ fallback
      downloadUrl = `${SUPABASE_STORAGE}/VodafoneFakka-v${latestVersion}.apk`;
    } else {
      // آخر حل — أحدث إصدار معروف في Supabase
      downloadUrl = `${SUPABASE_STORAGE}/VodafoneFakka-v3.0.249.apk`;
    }

    if (Capacitor.isNativePlatform()) {
      await Browser.open({ url: downloadUrl, windowName: '_system' });
    } else {
      window.open(downloadUrl, '_blank');
    }
  };
```

</action>

Old String: ```
/** فحص الحسابات المفقودة — profiles موجودة في DB بدون Auth record */
```

New String: ```
// ── جلب بيانات كاملة لمجموعة أجهزة مكررة (profiles + device_registry) ────
export interface DuplicateGroupProfile {
  id: string;
  username: string | null;
  email: string | null;
  full_name: string | null;
  phone: string | null;
  role: string;
  is_active: boolean;
  device_fp: string | null;
  created_at: string;
  // من fcm_tokens / device_registry
  device_model: string | null;
  platform: string | null;
  os_version: string | null;
  app_version: string | null;
}

export async function getDuplicateGroupProfiles(
  userIds: string[]
): Promise<{ data: DuplicateGroupProfile[]; error?: string }> {
  if (!userIds.length) return { data: [] };
  const { data: profiles, error: pErr } = await supabase
    .from('profiles')
    .select('id, username, email, full_name, phone, role, is_active, device_fp, created_at')
    .in('id', userIds);
  if (pErr) return { data: [], error: pErr.message };

  // جلب آخر token لكل مستخدم لمعرفة معلومات الجهاز
  const { data: tokens } = await supabase
    .from('fcm_tokens')
    .select('user_id, device_info, app_version')
    .in('user_id', userIds)
    .eq('is_active', true)
    .order('updated_at', { ascending: false });

  const tokenMap: Record<string, { device_model: string | null; platform: string | null; os_version: string | null; app_version: string | null }> = {};
  (tokens ?? []).forEach((t: { user_id: string; device_info?: { model?: string; platform?: string; os_version?: string }; app_version?: string | null }) => {
    if (!tokenMap[t.user_id]) {
      tokenMap[t.user_id] = {
        device_model: t.device_info?.model ?? null,
        platform:     t.device_info?.platform ?? null,
        os_version:   t.device_info?.os_version ?? null,
        app_version:  t.app_version ?? null,
      };
    }
  });

  const result: DuplicateGroupProfile[] = (profiles ?? []).map((p: {
    id: string; username: string | null; email: string | null; full_name: string | null;
    phone: string | null; role: string; is_active: boolean; device_fp: string | null; created_at: string;
  }) => ({
    ...p,
    ...(tokenMap[p.id] ?? { device_model: null, platform: null, os_version: null, app_version: null }),
  }));
  return { data: result };
}

/** حظر كل الحسابات المكررة ما عدا الحساب الرئيسي */
export async function banDuplicateAccounts(
  userIds: string[], primaryUserId?: string
): Promise<{ success: boolean; banned: number; errors: string[] }> {
  const targets = primaryUserId ? userIds.filter(id => id !== primaryUserId) : userIds;
  const errors: string[] = [];
  let banned = 0;
  await Promise.all(targets.map(async id => {
    const res = await toggleUserActive(id, false);
    if (res.error) errors.push(typeof res.error === 'string' ? res.error : String(res.error));
    else banned++;
  }));
  return { success: errors.length === 0, banned, errors };
}

/** حذف كل الحسابات المكررة ما عدا الحساب الرئيسي */
export async function deleteDuplicateAccounts(
  userIds: string[], primaryUserId?: string
): Promise<{ success: boolean; deleted: number; errors: string[] }> {
  const targets = primaryUserId ? userIds.filter(id => id !== primaryUserId) : userIds;
  const errors: string[] = [];
  let deleted = 0;
  await Promise.all(targets.map(async id => {
    const res = await deleteUserComplete(id);
    if (!res.success) errors.push(res.error ?? 'فشل الحذف');
    else deleted++;
  }));
  return { success: errors.length === 0, deleted, errors };
}
```

```
// صفحة إدارة الحسابات المكررة — القائمة الرئيسية v3.0.252
// ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
// تعرض قائمة مجموعات الأجهزة المكررة بشكل منظم
// الضغط على أي مجموعة → صفحة تفاصيل كاملة مع كل الإجراءات
import { useState, useEffect, useCallback } from 'react';
import { useNavigate } from 'react-router-dom';
import {
  Smartphone, RefreshCw, Loader2, Search,

function fmtDate(d?: string | null) {

function shortFp(fp?: string | null) {

// ── بطاقة مجموعة جهاز واحد ──────────────────────────────────────────────────
function GroupCard({ group, onClick }: { group: DuplicateDeviceGroup; onClick: () => void }) {
  const names = group.usernames.filter(Boolean);
  const displayNames = names.slice(0, 3).join('، ') + (names.length > 3 ? `، +${names.length - 3}` : '');

  return (
    <button
      onClick={onClick}
      className={`w-full text-right rounded-2xl border bg-card p-4 flex items-center gap-3 active:scale-[0.99] transition-all hover:border-primary/30 hover:shadow-md ${group.is_banned ? 'border-destructive/40' : 'border-border'}`}
    >
      {/* أيقونة */}
      <div className={`w-11 h-11 rounded-2xl flex items-center justify-center shrink-0 ${group.is_banned ? 'bg-destructive/10' : 'bg-warning/10'}`}>
        {group.is_banned
          ? <ShieldX className="w-5 h-5 text-destructive" />
          : <Smartphone className="w-5 h-5 text-warning" />
        }
      </div>

      {/* المحتوى */}
      <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
        <div className="flex items-center gap-2 mb-0.5">
          <p className="font-semibold text-sm truncate leading-snug">{displayNames || '—'}</p>
          {group.is_banned && (
            <Badge variant="destructive" className="text-[9px] px-1.5 h-4 shrink-0">محظور</Badge>
          )}
        </div>
        <div className="flex items-center gap-3 text-xs text-muted-foreground">
          <span className="flex items-center gap-1">
            <Users className="w-3 h-3" />
            {group.user_count} حسابات
          </span>
          <span className="truncate font-mono">{shortFp(group.device_fp ?? group.hardware_hash)}</span>
        </div>
        <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground mt-0.5">
          آخر نشاط: {fmtDate(group.last_seen)}
        </p>
      </div>

      {/* سهم */}
      <ChevronLeft className="w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground shrink-0" />
    </button>
  );
}

// ── الصفحة الرئيسية ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
type TabId = 'duplicates' | 'banned_accounts' | 'device_bans';

export default function AdminDuplicateAccounts() {
  const navigate = useNavigate();
  const [tab, setTab]             = useState<TabId>('duplicates');
  const [loading, setLoading]     = useState(true);
  const [search, setSearch]       = useState('');

  const [duplicates, setDuplicates]     = useState<DuplicateDeviceGroup[]>([]);
  const [deviceBans, setDeviceBans]     = useState<DeviceBan[]>([]);
  const [bannedAccs, setBannedAccs]     = useState<BannedAccount[]>([]);

  const load = useCallback(async () => {
    setLoading(true);
    try {
      const [d, b, a] = await Promise.all([
        getDuplicateDevices(),
        getDeviceBans(),
        getBannedAccounts(),
      ]);
      if (d.success) setDuplicates(d.data);
      if (b.success) setDeviceBans(b.data);
      setBannedAccs(a.data ?? []);
    } catch (e) {
      toast.error('فشل التحميل');
    } finally {
      setLoading(false);
    }
  }, []);

  useEffect(() => { load(); }, [load]);

  // ── فلترة ──
  const filteredDups = duplicates.filter(g => {
    const q = search.toLowerCase();
    return !q
      || g.usernames.some(u => u?.toLowerCase().includes(q))
      || g.phones.some(p => p?.toLowerCase().includes(q))
      || (g.device_fp ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q)
      || (g.hardware_hash ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q);
  });
  const filteredBannedAccs = bannedAccs.filter(a => {
    const q = search.toLowerCase();
    return !q || (a.username ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q) || (a.phone ?? '').includes(q);
  });
  const filteredDeviceBans = deviceBans.filter(b => {
    const q = search.toLowerCase();
    return !q
      || (b.ban_reason ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q)
      || b.associated_usernames?.some(u => u.toLowerCase().includes(q))
      || (b.device_fp ?? '').toLowerCase().includes(q);
  });

  // ── إحصائيات ──
  const stats = [
    { label: 'أجهزة مكررة',      val: duplicates.length,                      icon: Smartphone,  color: 'text-warning'     },
    { label: 'حسابات محظورة',    val: bannedAccs.length,                       icon: Ban,         color: 'text-destructive'  },
    { label: 'حظر الأجهزة',      val: deviceBans.filter(b => b.is_active).length, icon: ShieldX, color: 'text-destructive'  },
    { label: 'أجهزة محظورة نشطة',val: duplicates.filter(d => d.is_banned).length, icon: AlertTriangle, color: 'text-orange-400' },
  ];

  const TABS: { id: TabId; label: string; count: number }[] = [
    { id: 'duplicates',      label: 'أجهزة مكررة',   count: duplicates.length },
    { id: 'banned_accounts', label: 'حسابات محظورة', count: bannedAccs.length },
    { id: 'device_bans',     label: 'حظر الأجهزة',   count: deviceBans.filter(b => b.is_active).length },
  ];

  const handleGroupClick = (g: DuplicateDeviceGroup) => {
    // تمرير البيانات عبر state لتجنب encoding مشاكل في URL
    const key = g.device_fp ?? g.hardware_hash ?? g.device_id ?? '';
    navigate(`/admin/duplicate-accounts/${encodeURIComponent(key)}`, { state: { group: g } });
  };

  return (
    <AdminShell
      title="الحسابات المكررة"
      subtitle="كشف وإدارة الأجهزة ذات الحسابات المتعددة"
      breadcrumbs={[{ label: 'الإدارة', href: '/admin' }, { label: 'الحسابات المكررة' }]}
      actions={
        <Button variant="outline" size="sm" onClick={load} disabled={loading} className="gap-1.5">
          {loading ? <Loader2 className="w-3.5 h-3.5 animate-spin" /> : <RefreshCw className="w-3.5 h-3.5" />}
          تحديث
        </Button>
      }
    >
      {/* إحصائيات */}
      <div className="grid grid-cols-2 md:grid-cols-4 gap-3 mb-4">
        {stats.map(s => (
          <div key={s.label} className="rounded-2xl border bg-card p-3 flex items-center gap-3">
            <div className="w-9 h-9 rounded-xl bg-muted flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">
              <s.icon className={`w-4 h-4 ${s.color}`} />
            </div>
            <div>
              <p className="text-xl font-bold leading-none">{s.val}</p>
              <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground mt-0.5">{s.label}</p>
            </div>
          </div>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* فحص شامل */}
      <div className="mb-4">
        <Button
          variant="outline"
          className="gap-2 w-full md:w-auto border-primary/30 text-primary hover:bg-primary/5"
          onClick={load}
        >
          <ScanSearch className="w-4 h-4" />
          فحص شامل للأجهزة المكررة
        </Button>
      </div>

      {/* بحث */}
      <div className="relative mb-4">
        <Search className="absolute right-3 top-1/2 -translate-y-1/2 w-4 h-4 text-muted-foreground" />
        <Input
          value={search}
          onChange={e => setSearch(e.target.value)}
          placeholder="ابحث بالاسم أو الجهاز أو الهاتف..."
          className="pr-9 h-11 rounded-xl"
        />
      </div>

      {/* تبويبات */}
      <div className="flex gap-2 mb-4 overflow-x-auto pb-1">
        {TABS.map(t => (
          <button
            key={t.id}
            onClick={() => setTab(t.id)}
            className={`flex items-center gap-2 px-4 py-2 rounded-xl text-sm font-medium shrink-0 transition-colors ${
              tab === t.id ? 'bg-primary text-primary-foreground' : 'bg-muted text-muted-foreground hover:bg-muted/70'
            }`}
          >
            {t.label}
            {t.count > 0 && (
              <span className={`text-xs px-1.5 py-0.5 rounded-full ${tab === t.id ? 'bg-white/20' : 'bg-background'}`}>
                {t.count}
              </span>
            )}
          </button>
        ))}
      </div>

      {/* المحتوى */}
      {loading ? (
        <div className="flex justify-center items-center py-16">
          <Loader2 className="w-7 h-7 animate-spin text-muted-foreground" />
        </div>
      ) : (
        <>
          {/* ── أجهزة مكررة ── */}
          {tab === 'duplicates' && (
            <div className="space-y-3">
              {filteredDups.length === 0 ? (
                <div className="text-center py-12 text-muted-foreground">
                  <ShieldCheck className="w-10 h-10 mx-auto mb-3 opacity-40" />
                  <p>لا توجد أجهزة مكررة</p>
                </div>
              ) : (
                filteredDups.map((g, i) => (
                  <GroupCard key={i} group={g} onClick={() => handleGroupClick(g)} />
                ))
              )}
            </div>
          )}

          {/* ── حسابات محظورة ── */}
          {tab === 'banned_accounts' && (
            <div className="space-y-3">
              {filteredBannedAccs.length === 0 ? (
                <div className="text-center py-12 text-muted-foreground">
                  <ShieldCheck className="w-10 h-10 mx-auto mb-3 opacity-40" />
                  <p>لا توجد حسابات محظورة</p>
                </div>
              ) : filteredBannedAccs.map(a => (
                <div key={a.id} className="rounded-2xl border border-destructive/30 bg-card p-4 flex items-center gap-3">
                  <div className="w-10 h-10 rounded-xl bg-destructive/10 flex items-center justify-center shrink-0">
                    <Ban className="w-4 h-4 text-destructive" />
                  </div>
                  <div className="flex-1 min-w-0">
                    <p className="font-semibold text-sm truncate">{a.username ?? '—'}</p>
                    <p className="text-xs text-muted-foreground truncate">{a.phone ?? a.email ?? '—'}</p>
                    <p className="text-[10px] text-muted-foreground">
                      {a.updated_at ? format(new Date(a.updated_at), 'dd MMM yyyy', { locale: ar }) : '—'}
                    </p>
                  </div>
                  <Button
                    size="sm"
                    variant="outline"
                    className="shrink-0 text-xs h-8"
                    onClick={() => navigate(`/admin/users/${a.id}`)}
                  >
                    عرض
                  </Button>
                </div>
              ))}
            </div>
          )}

          {/* ── حظر الأجهزة ── */}
          {tab === 'device_bans' && (
            <div className="space-y-3">
              {filteredDeviceBans.length === 0 ? (
                <div className="text-center py-12 text-muted-foreground">
                  <ShieldCheck className="w-10 h-10 mx-auto mb-3 opacity-40" />
                  <p>لا توجد أجهزة محظورة</p>
                </div>
              ) : filteredDeviceBans.map(b => (
                <div key={b.id} className={`rounded-2xl border bg-card p-4 ${b.is_active ? 'border-destructive/40' : 'border-border opacity-60'}`}>
                  <div className="flex items-center gap-3 mb-2">
```
